```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    a = ()
    n = len(lst)
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i, n):
            if ((lst[i] == lst[j]) and (i != j)):
                a += (lst[j],)
            else:
                continue
    c = a[:(- 1)]
    b = lst[::(- 1)]
    for i in range(len(c)):
        b.remove(c[i])
    d = b[::(- 1)]
    return d
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    n = []
    for ref_i in lst:
        if ref_i not in n:
            n.append(ref_i)
    return n
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    a = ()
    n = len(lst)
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i, n):
            if lst[i] == lst[j] and i != j:
                a += (lst[j],)
            else:
                continue
    c = a[:(-1)]
    b = lst[::(-1)]
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    lst.sort()
    i = 0
    while (i < len(lst)):
        if (i == (len(lst) - 1)):
            break
        elif (lst[i] == lst[(i + 1)]):
            lst.remove(lst[i])
        else:
            i += 1
    return lst
```

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new_lst = [lst[0]]
    if (lst == []):
        return []
    for i in range(len(lst)):
        a = lst[i]
        for h in range(i, len(lst)):
            if (a != lst[h]):
                ele = lst[h]
                if (ele in new_lst):
                    continue
                new_lst.append(ele)
    return new_lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    for i in range((l - 1)):
        for j in range((i + 1), l):
            if (lst[i] == lst[j]):
                del lst[j]
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    i = 0
    while i < l:
        j = i + 1
        while j < l:
            if lst[i] == lst[j]:
                del lst[j]
                l -= 1
            else:
                j += 1
        i += 1
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    listt = lst.copy()
    listt.reverse()
    for element in listt:
        if (listt.count(element) > 1):
            listt.remove(element)
    listt.reverse()
    return listt
```

the corrected code is incorrect

Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    i = 0
    while i < l:
        j = i + 1
        while j < l:
            if lst[i] == lst[j]:
                del lst[j]
                l -= 1
            else:
                j += 1
        i += 1
    return lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    count = 0
    rev_lst = lst.copy()
    rev_lst.reverse()
    ori_len = len(lst)
    new_lst = lst.copy()
    for i in range(ori_len):
        if (rev_lst[i] in rev_lst[(i + 1):]):
            new_lst.pop(((ori_len - i) - 1))
    return new_lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    result = []
    for x in lst:

            result.append(x)
    return result
```

wrong_3_218.py
structure mutation
------------
User-defined identifiers from the incorrect code:
- remove_extras
- lst
- i
- new
- curr
- ele

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    i = 0
    new = []
    while (i <= len(lst)):
        curr = lst[i]
        for ele in lst:
            if (ele == curr):
                continue
            new += [ele]
        lst = new.copy()
        new = []
        i += 1
    return lst
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    newlist = []
    for ele in lst:
        if (ele not in newlist):
            newlist.append(ele)
    return newlist
```

wrong_3_286.py

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    for element in lst:
        while (lst.count(element) > 1):
            lst.remove(element)
            if (lst.count(element) == 1):
                break
    return lst
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    ref_newlist = []
    for i in lst:
        if (i not in ref_newlist):
            ref_newlist.append(i)
    return ref_newlist
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    lst.reverse()
    ref_newlist = []
    for i in lst:
        if (lst.count(i) > 1):
            j = 0
            while (j < i):
                lst.remove(i)
                j += 1
        if (i not in ref_newlist):
            ref_newlist.append(i)
    lst.reverse()
    return lst
```

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    i = 0
    new = []
    while (i <= len(lst)):
        curr = lst[i]
        for ele in lst:
            if (ele == curr):
                continue
            new += [ele]
        lst = new.copy()
        new = []
        i += 1
    return lst
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new = []
    for ele in lst:
        if ele not in new:
            new.append(ele)
    return new
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    for i in range(l):
        for j in range(i + 1, l):
            if lst[i] == lst[j]:
                del lst[j]
                l -= 1
    return lst
```

the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    l = len(lst)
    i = 0
    while i < l:
        j = i + 1
        while j < l:
            if lst[i] == lst[j]:
                del lst[j]
                l -= 1
            else:
                j += 1
        i += 1
    return lst
```

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    i = 0
    new = []
    while (i < len(lst)):
        curr = lst[i]
        for ele in lst:
            if (ele == curr):
                continue
            new += [ele]
        lst = new.copy()
        new = []
        i += 1
    return lst
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new = []
    for ele in lst:
        if ele not in new:
            new.append(ele)
    return new
```

```python
    lst_copy = lst.copy()
    lst_copy.reverse()
    ori_len = len(lst_copy)
```

User-defined identifiers from the incorrect code:
- remove_extras
- remove_multiple

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    for i in lst:
        remove_multiple(i, lst)
    return lst

def remove_multiple(n, lst):
    if lst.count(n) == 1:
        return lst
    else:
        lst.reverse()
        lst.remove(n)
        lst.reverse()
        return remove_multiple(n, lst)
```

wrong_3_212.py

User-defined identifiers from the incorrect code:
- remove_extras
- lst
- position
- helper

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    def position(i):
        n = len(lst)
        for j in range(n):
            if (lst[j] == i):
                return j
    
    def helper(start, i):
        for k in lst[start:]:
            if (k == i):
                lst.remove(k)
    
    for i in lst:
        index = position(i)
        helper((index + 1), i)
    
    return lst
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    def position(i):
        n = len(lst)
        for j in range(n):
            if (lst[j] == i):
                return j
    def helper(start, i):
        for k in lst[start:]:
            if (k == i):
                lst.remove(k)
        else:
            pass
    new_lst = lst.copy()
    for i in new_lst:
        index = position(i)
        helper((index + 1), i)
    return lst
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new_lst = []
    for ref_i in lst:
        if ref_i not in new_lst:
            new_lst.append(ref_i)
    return new_lst
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    sub_list = []
    for elem in lst:
        if (elem not in lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]):
            return lst
        elif (elem in lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]):
            sub_list += lst[(lst.index(elem) + 1):]
            while (elem in sub_list):
                sub_list.remove(elem)
            return(lst[:(lst.index(elem) + 1)] + sub_list)
```

the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    ref_newlist = []
    for ref_i in lst:
        if (ref_i not in ref_newlist):
            ref_newlist.append(ref_i)
    return ref_newlist
```

```python
def remove_extras(lst):
    new_lst = lst
    for i in lst:
        n = new_lst.count(i)
        while True:
            if (n <= 1):
                break
            else:
                new_lst.remove(i)
                n -= 1
    return new_lst
```
